hone ke baavjood jivan main safalataa praapt kar lete hanchhote talave- jarurat se zyada chote talave vyakti ko maansik chintaa main daal dete hai- aise log kaaphi sangharsh ke baad hi jivan main kuch paa sakate hai- aam taur par jaise-jaise umr badhati jaati he, vaise-vaise chijen behatar hoti hansaamaanya talave- saamaanya talave zyada kuch soochna nahin dete- iske liye saamaanya talave ke pair ke anguuthe ko dekhnaa hoga- talave ke paas anguuthe kii rekha acchhee ho to saamaanya talave bhi achche prabhaav dete hankya kahati hai talave or pairon kii anguliyaan?- pairon kaa angootha, agar bagal vaali anguli se chota ho to yah bhagya main vruddhi karata he- agar pair kii sabase choti anguli kaaphi choti ho, yaa isamen nakhun bahut hi chota ho to vaivaahik jivan kharaab hota he- agar pair kii sabase choti anguli lambi ho to vyakti ko dhan kaa abhaav nahin hota- agar pairon kii anguliyaan tedi medhi ho to vyakti kii kismat main do vivaah kaa yoga ban jaataa he- agar pair kaa angootha zyada hi bada ho to yah beemaari kaa lakshan hota hashiridy vaale sai baba kii karen upasna, puri hogi har manokamanakya kahata he talave kaa rang?- talave kaa rang swaabhaavik or saaf ho to  sau din yah tay karne ke liye kaaphi nahin he ki is kanoon main kaise sudhaar kiya janaa chahie, lekin ise lagu karne se to roka hi ja saktaa he taaki skool chalate rahen
 Obviously, this will cause ruckus
 rajdhani main sarkari shikshakon kaa taqatvar kunba or unke saathi shor machayenge
 But the step which will make the situation more interesting is that the subsidy on petroleum products should be abolished
 bahut pehle se yah saaf ho chukaa he ki ye chijen hamaare paryaavaran ke liye buree hai or hamen peeche dhakelne vaali hai
 To make this decision a little more enjoyable, the government should also announce that 50% of the existing petroleum subsidy will be spent on universal cash transfer
 ek saal main kar daalencash transfar ke liye kisi lambii-chaudee vyavastha kii jarurat nahin he
 Giving everyone a UID or unique identity card will make it easier to ensure that no one can take advantage of it twice
 agar har kisi ke paas apana bank khaataa hoga to transfar karnaa aasaan ho jayega
